1975     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a92b2bb22b7d9a7224e120efa1efaebe8}{SLJIT\_EQUAL\_F64}:
1976     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a18d216b789f74102b91592f819b9d136}{SLJIT\_NOT\_EQUAL\_F64}:
1977     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a35e83b6ebf61512403371b2e7e5b4434}{SLJIT\_LESS\_F64}:
1978     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a1eed18ab67ea65b0f1bb664450fd9ec5}{SLJIT\_GREATER\_EQUAL\_F64}:
1979     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a368a97a0ac86e77fb65a8426abac809f}{SLJIT\_UNORDERED\_F64}:
1980     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a7d0fe67333f98ede0922883186ba5c10}{SLJIT\_ORDERED\_F64}:
1981         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a751ef36dde977c4f12b34bda6b04d8ca}{CFC1} | \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a23cd8a4302f377385c79a86557f5395e}{TA}(dst\_ar) | \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a48a4f47110c95575b045cf717bf99d14}{DA}(
      \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_ae128ae3d48e0430c88085ba0d0086c5b}{FCSR\_REG}), dst\_ar));
1982         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a391959af0568008f17f41df83486de19}{SRL} | \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a23cd8a4302f377385c79a86557f5395e}{TA}(dst\_ar) | \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a48a4f47110c95575b045cf717bf99d14}{DA}(dst\_ar) | 
      \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a26a65b27a11d7bf29e02c52a6893aeea}{SH\_IMM}(23), dst\_ar));

      \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_ad43e91ae83de424cf93e1adfa61c5227}{IMM}(1), dst\_ar));
1984         src\_ar = dst\_ar;
1985         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1986

1988         src\_ar = \hyperlink{sljitNativeMIPS__common_8c_a2e8492fa6b719d115bf69365d96bb35b}{OTHER\_FLAG};
1989         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1990     \}
1991

2004     \}
